    JAP_the_pandemic_worsens_mission = {
	    icon = generic_coronavirus
		allowed = {
		    tag = JAP
		}
		visible = {
		    has_country_flag = JAP_coronavirus_strikes
		}
		available = {
		    has_country_flag = JAP_dealt_with_coronavirus
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 85
		timeout_effect = { 
		    JAP_increase_coronavirus = yes
		    activate_mission = JAP_the_pandemic_worsens_mission
			if = {
			    limit = {
					has_government = conservative
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
				    var = JAP_election_approval_rating_ldp_var_temp
					value = -0.01
				}
				JAP_add_election_approval_rating_ldp = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = conservative
						popularity = -0.01
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

JAP_jietai_cat = {
	JAP_increase_financing_for_rearmament  = {
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_rearmament_changed_recently
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = JAP_continued_rearmament_idea_high2
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_continue_rearmament
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 1
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_rearmament_changed_recently
			JAP_increase_rearmament = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = JAP_rearmament_changed_recently
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	JAP_reduce_financing_for_rearmament = {
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_rearmament_changed_recently
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = JAP_continued_rearmament_idea_low2
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_continue_rearmament
		}
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 60
		days_re_enable = 1
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = JAP_rearmament_changed_recently
			JAP_decrease_rearmament = yes
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = JAP_rearmament_changed_recently
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
